# Lembar Contek Emoji

[![Pemutakhiran](https://github.com/ikatyang/emoji-cheat-sheet/workflows/Up%20to%20Date/badge.svg)](https://github.com/ikatyang/emoji-cheat-sheet/actions?query=workflow%3A%22Up+to+Date%22)

Referensi Lembar Contek Emoji GitHub ini via [GitHub Emoji API](https://api.github.com/emojis) dan [Unicode Full Emoji List](https://unicode.org/emoji/charts/full-emoji-list.html).

<h4 dir="auto"><a aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/ikatyang/emoji-cheat-sheet/blob/master/README.md#subdivision-flag" id="user-content-subdivision-flag"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16"></svg></a></h4>

<h4 dir="auto">Subdivision Flag</h4>

<table>
	<thead>
		<tr>
			<th>&nbsp;</th>
			<th align="center">ico</th>
			<th>shortcode</th>
			<th align="center">ico</th>
			<th>shortcode</th>
			<th>&nbsp;</th>
		</tr>
	</thead>
